layout: "post"
title: "The circle"
date: "2018-05-01"
agda: true
toc: true
categories: type-theory
---

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: . equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

I gave a talk giving one solution using the flattening lemma:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="616" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="621" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="628" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">2018-07-06-mini-hott</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  S¹ type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point
and one no trivial path called path as we show in the following
picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png)
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

## `pS` type

![path](/assets/ipe-images/tour-type.png)
*Figure 2. `pS` Type.*

## Equivalences

### Lemma 1

{: .equation }

  $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**.

Let us define the outgoing functions:

The proof of the homotopy $$ f' ∘ g' \sim \mathsf{id}$$.

          <a id="8388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#5179" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="8393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#2058" class="Function">pS₀</a>
        <a id="8405" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7833" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of the homotopy $$g' ∘ f' \sim \mathsf{id}$$:

- Action on paths of pairs

### Lemma 3

{: .equation}
  $$
    \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS
  $$

  where $$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

      <a id="13693" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13693" class="Postulate">lemma-ap-f-γ₀₁</a> <a id="13708" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13710" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#8111" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="13713" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13080" class="Function">f</a> <a id="13715" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13716" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#16337" class="Function">pair=</a> <a id="13722" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13723" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1031" class="Postulate">loop</a> <a id="13728" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#2329" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13730" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13134" class="Function">γ₀₁</a><a id="13733" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="13736" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#5044" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="13739" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#2133" class="Postulate">p₁₀</a>

Let us prove the homotopies:
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13854" class="Comment">-- Homotopy</a>
    <a id="13870" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13870" class="Function">f-g</a> <a id="13874" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13876" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13080" class="Function">f</a> <a id="13878" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4004" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="13880" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13353" class="Function">g</a> <a id="13882" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#18287" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="13884" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3527" class="Function">id</a>
